< Review>
Went here because of the 4.5 star review but was quickly disappointed. A brief description of my experience.
1) Waited 20 mins to be seen but was told only a 15 min wait
2) Linda did my gel manicure (I don't reccomend her).To remove the old gel she put waaaay too much acetone in the foil so that my fingertips were almost frozen before she got to them.
3) The worst part of my experience was when she was cleaning the cuticles. She was rushing and kept nicking into my skin causing bleeding on every cuticle bed. In 20 years of doing my nails I have never had so many lacerations and so much bleeding on all my fingers from cleaning the cuticles. When I brought this to her attention, instead of an apology she blamed my nails for causing the bleeding. Never an acknowledgement or apology for this.
4) With all the cuts on my fingers from her sloppy work, for the rest of the session, whenever she would rub my nails with acetone or alcohol, they would sting even further. She would rub it aggressively, rushing to  I'm not sure where,  and causing even more pain.
5) The whole expereince was quite a nightmare. Manicures are supposed to be a somewhat relaxing experience; not make shift torture chambers which is exactly what this was.
6) The only reason I gave 1 star instead of 0 is the price was reasonable.
7) My fingers will be hurting for days from this, and stinging every time I wash my hands or use alchohol cleanser (which I do quite frequently as I'm a medical professional)
8) Would not reccomend coming here unless you enjoy being tortured for an hour and having it last for a week or 2 until your cuticle beds heal.<//Review>
